 Chidambaram is seen trying very hard to revive the economy
 iske maddenjar ve saarvajanik kshetra ke bainkon ke pramukhon ke saath baithak karne vaale hai
 In view of the slowdown in economic growth, Finance Minister p Chidambaram may ask banks to give more loans in a meeting with the heads of public sector banks on 18 March
 aadhikarik sutron ne bataaya ki is baithak ke agenda main pratyaksh nakadi antaran, parisampatti kii ghatati gunvattta, rin main vruddhi aadi shaamil hai
 In view of the slowdown in the economy, non-performing assets (npas) of banks have been increasing for the past several months
 bhartiya state bank, punjab neshnal bank or central bank aaf india samet kuch sarkari bainkon kaa enpie disambar 2012 tak kul parisampatti ke chaar fisad ke str ko paar kar gaya he
 As of December 2012, the total npas of public sector banks increased by Rs 47,091 crore to Rs 1,84,193 crore from Rs 1,37,102 crore in March 2012
 sutron ke mutabik is baithak main sookshm, laghu or majhole upkram (emsamai), krishi, buniyadi dhaancha or awaas kshetra ko diya jane vaale rin ke vistaar par bhi vichaar kiya jayega
 The meeting will take place a day before the mid-quarter review of the Reserve Bank of India's monetary policy
 ummid kii ja rahi he ki rigerv bank vruddhi ko protsaahan ke liye byaaj daron main katautee kar saktaa he
 Earlier in the third quarter review of monetary policy on 29 January, the central bank raised policy rates to 0
 25 fisad kii katautee kii thi
 Apart from this, the cash reserve ratio (CRR) was also cut down, which gave banks an additional cash of Rs 18,000 crore for lending and meeting their other needs
 dilli police ne car chori karne vaali ek aisi gang ko pakadaa he jo maang ke mutabik car chori karti thi
 Before the robbery, a photo of the car was sent to the gang leader on whatsapp
 you-tub ke video se chori ke tareeke siikhe jate the
 The stolen goods were purchased from Amazon and then the car theft in 10 minutes
 ek vaahan chor ne demo bataaya ki vah kaise car chori karata he
 Whatever the safety arrangements in the cars, it is only a 10-minute task for this person equipped with the technical knowledge to steal
 usne hamaare saamne mahaj 10 minute main car start kar di
 According to DMP Romil Bania of south-east Delhi, every big car company makes claims of better security features in their cars these days, but after getting caught by this gang, it is clear that whatever security features are there, it is possible to fail this gang
 The game is left handed
 police ne vaahan chori karne vaali is hitech gang ke chaar logon aamir,safar,sagir or shoeb khan ko giraftaar kiya he
 While their leader, the master power, is still absconding
 police ke mutabik inke chori karne kaa tarika bilkul alag tha
 Based on the demand, a member of this gang used to Reiki first and send a photo of the same car to his boss on whatsapp
 hari jhandi milte hi us car ke suraksha intjaamon ko fail karne ke video gang ke log utyub par dekhte the
 After this, similar to stealing, such as fake keys, key memory cards and key programmers were purchased from Amazon
 is gang main alag-alag companiyon kii car chori karne ke liye alag-alag export hai
 According to the police, the gang people first cut the horn wire from under the car
 phir peeche kaa glass todakar daravaaje kholte the
 After that, we used to take the part out of the drill from where the key is started to start the car
 iske baad kii programmer ko car ke dimag yani isiem se jodate the or car kaa puraa software copy kar lete the
 After this, the same software was put in the memory card of the fake key and the car started with the same key
 tippaniyan The information about the car which is equipped with GPS was obtained from a device with a laser light
 use ye aam taur par chori nahin karte the
 According to police, Sagir's gang has more than 50 expert boys who have been stealing since 2005
 takneekee chori main maahir in ladakon main koi bhi padhaa likhaa nahin he
 Police have recovered 16 expensive vehicles from them

 Stock market investors will keep an eye on the Winter Session of Parliament next week and important data released by the government
 sansad kaa sheetakaaleen adhiveshan 22 navambar se jari he
 Many important economic bills are to be introduced in Parliament
 inamen pension vidheyak, beemaa vidheyak or banking kanoon (sanshodhan) vidheyak-2011 pramukh hai
 The Insurance Bill provides for raising the foreign direct investment (FDI) limit from 26 per cent to 49 per cent
 pension vidheyak main gharelu fund manageron main 49 fisadi tak epadiai seemaa ko anumati die jane kaa praavdhaan he
 The Bank Laws (amendment) Bill 2011 provides for the elimination of the maximum voting limit of 10 per cent in private banks and the increase in government banks from one per cent to 10 per cent
 iske alaava isamen bhartiya rigerv bank ko adhik adhikaar bhi diya gaya he
 The Reserve Bank of India has asked the government to first pass the Banking Laws (amendment) Bill 2011 in the House, only then it will consider the issue of granting new bank licenses
 kendriya sankhyikee sanghathan agle saptaah kai mahatvapurn aankade jari karegaa
 Industrial production data for the month of October will be released on Wednesday 12 December
 november maheene ke liye thok keemton par aadhaarit mahangaai dar kaa aankada 14 disambar ko jari kiya jayega
 The country's companies will start depositing advance tax for the third quarter from December 15
 niveshak isse companiyon ke pradarshan ke mahatvapurn sanket le sakate hai
 Advance tax is deposited in four installments from 15 June, 15 September, 15 December and 15 March
 tippaniyan Next week, Bharti Infratel and PC Jeweler are coming out with their primary public offering (IPO)
 bhartiya airtel kii sahaayak company bharti infratel kaa ipo mangalvaar 11 disambar ko khulegaa
 The IPO price range has been kept from Rs 210 to Rs 240 per share
 ipo shuukravaar 14 disambar ko band hoga
 PC Jeweler's IPO will open on Monday 10 December and will close on Wednesday 12 December
 ipo main share kaa mulya dayera 125 rupee se 135 rupee rakhaa gaya he
 Winter session of Parliament continues from 22 November
 kai mahatvapurn aarthik vidheyak sansad main pesh kiye jane vaale hai
 These include the Pension Bill, Insurance Bill and Banking Laws (amendment) Bill-2011
 beemaa vidheyak main pratyaksh videshi nivesh (epadiai) kii seemaa ko 26 fisadi se badhaakar 49 fisadi kiye jane kaa praavdhaan he
 The pension bill provides for allowing FDI limit up to 49 per cent in domestic fund managers
 bank kanoon (sanshodhan) vidheyak 2011 main nijee bainkon main adhiktam matdaan seemaa 10 fisadi ko samaapt karne or sarkari bainkon main ek fisadi se badhaakar 10 fisadi kiye jane kaa praavdhaan he
 Apart from this, the Reserve Bank of India has also been given more powers
 bhartiya rigerv bank ne sarkaar se kaha he ki pehle vah banking kanoon (sanshodhan) vidheyak 2011 ko sadan main paarit karaae, tabhi vah nae bank license dene ke mudde par vichaar karegaa
 The Central Statistical Organization will release several important figures next week
 buudhvaar 12 disambar ko oktober maheene kaa audyogic utpaadan aankada jari kiya jayega
 The data on inflation based on wholesale prices for the month of November will be released on 14 December
 desh kii companiyaan 15 disambar se teesri timahi kaa agrim kar jamaa karnaa shuru kar dengi
 Investors can take important indications of the performance of companies from this
 agrim kar chaar kishton main 15 june, 15 sitambar, 15 disambar or 15 march se jamaa kii jaati he
 The comments agle saptaah bharti infratel or pisi jeweler apane praathmik saarvajanik nirgam (ipo) lekar aa rahi he
 The IPO of Bharti Infratel, a subsidiary of Bharti Airtel, will open on Tuesday 11 December
 ipo kaa mulya dayera 210 rupee se 240 rupee prati share rakhaa gaya he
 The IPO will close on Friday 14 December
 pisi jeweler kaa ipo somvaar 10 disambar ko khulegaa or buudhvaar 12 disambar ko band hoga
 The price range of the shares in the IPO has been kept from Rs 125 to Rs 135

 dilli main mukhya nirvachan ayog ne ravivaar ko kaha ki iviem ke saath koi bhi chhedchhad nahin kar saktaa hai
 They cannot be manipulated even during construction
 electronic voting mashiinon (iviem) kii vishwasaneeyata ko lekar vipaksh ke jor-shor se sawaal khadaa karne par ayog ne bataaya ki apana vichaar rakhane ke liye usne aksar puche jane vaale sawaalon kii ek FAQ suchi saarvajanik kii he
 Recently, the Commission issued two statements defending the machines and this is the third FAQ attempt to answer those who doubt the reliability of the machines
 FAQ main jin prashnon kaa ullekh he, unamem pehla sawaal he : mashin ko hack kiya ja saktaa he yaa nahin? ayog kaa jawaab he : nahin
 The Election Commission stated that the M1 model of EVM was built by the year 2006 and included all the necessary technologies that no one could hack, contrary to the claims of some people
 iviem ke em2 model ko varsh 2006 ke baad nirmit kiya gaya tha or varsh 2012 tak isamen atirikt suraksha suvidhaayen shaamil kii gayi thim
 The ECI-EVM computers are no longer operated, the election panel said
 ye aisi mashin hai jinhen naa to internet se or naa hi anya network se joda jaataa he
 So there is no possibility of it being hacked from any remote device
 
 
 saath hi isamen koi frequency resiver yaa wireles ke liye dicoder athwa anya kisi gaiyr-iviem yantra yaa upkaran se jodne ke liye koi bahya hardware port nahin he
 However, the commission also dismissed questions suspected of manipulation by EVM manufacturers
 ayog ne kaha, yah sambhav nahin he kyonki varsh 2006 se iviem alag alag varsh main nirmit kii gayin or alag alag rajyon main bheji gayin
 Producer - Bharat Electronics Limited, Bangalore (BEL) and Electronics Corporation of India Limited, Hyderabad (ECIL) many years ago could not know who would contest in a particular constituency and the order of candidates on the ballot unit
 ayog se yah poocha gaya ki aakhir america or europea sangh jaise viksit deshon ne iviem ko kyon nahin apanaaya or kuch ne iskaa istemaal band kyon kar diya
 In response, the Commission said that the problem with these machines came because these countries had made them computer controlled and connected to the network, due to which the possibility of hacking increased
